Information about object: Boulder

Sprite: Boulder_Sprite
Solid: false
Visible: true
Depth: -6
Persistent: false
Parent: <no parent>
Mask: Colission_Mask

Create Event:
execute code:if (place_meeting(x,y,Tunnling_Bomb_Object))
{
    sprite_index = Tunnling_Bomb_Sprite
    rock_tunnle = 1
}

if (place_meeting(x,y,Dimond_Bomb_Object))
{
    sprite_index = Dimond_Bomb_Sprite
    rock_tunnle = 1
    dimond_tunnle = 1
}

if (place_meeting(x,y,Concreet_Bomb_Object))
{
    sprite_index = Concreet_Bomb_Sprite
    rock_tunnle = 1
    dimond_tunnle = 1
    concreet_tunnle = 1
}

if (place_meeting(x,y,Nuclear_Bomb_Object))
{
    sprite_index = Nuclear_Bomb_Sprite
    nuclear = 1
}

if (place_meeting(x,y,J_Bomb_Object))
{
    sprite_index = J_Bomb_Sprite
    j_bomb = 1
}

if (place_meeting(x,y,Time_Bomb_Object))
{
    time_bomb = 1
    countdown = 5
}

Destroy Event:
execute code:global.boulder_sound_playing = false

Alarm Event for alarm 0:
execute code:if (y == teleport_y) script_execute(M_Detonate)

Alarm Event for alarm 1:
execute code:if (y == teleport_y) script_execute(J_Detonate)

Alarm Event for alarm 2:
execute code:global.boulder_sound_playing = false

 Step Event:
execute script Time_Bomb_Script with arguments (0,0,0,0,0)

End Step Event:
execute script Boulder_Fall with arguments (0,0,0,0,0)

Collision Event with object Rock:
if rock_tunnle is larger than 0
      for other object: change the instance into object Yellow, not performing events

Collision Event with object Dimond:
if dimond_tunnle is larger than 0
      for other object: change the instance into object Yellow, not performing events

Collision Event with object Concreet:
if concreet_tunnle is larger than 0
      for other object: change the instance into object Yellow, not performing events

Mouse Event for Left Button:
execute script Time_Bomb_Set with arguments (0,0,0,0,0)

Mouse Event for Right Button:
execute code:if (global.cheats) instance_destroy()

Draw Event:
execute code:if (time_bomb>0) 
{
    draw_sprite(Time_Bomb_Sprite,countdown,x,y)
}
else if (j_bomb>0)
{
    draw_sprite(J_Bomb_Sprite,0,x,y)
}
else if (nuclear>0)
{
    draw_sprite(Nuclear_Bomb_Sprite,0,x,y)
}
else if (concreet_tunnle>0)
{
    draw_sprite(Concreet_Bomb_Sprite,0,x,y)
}
else if (dimond_tunnle>0)
{
    draw_sprite(Dimond_Bomb_Sprite,0,x,y)
}
else if (rock_tunnle>0)
{
    draw_sprite(Tunnling_Bomb_Sprite,0,x,y)
}
else 
{
    draw_sprite(Boulder_Sprite,0,x,y)
}

    if (global.message_type==20) script_execute(B_help)
}

 Step Event:
execute code:Music_Script()
Player_Win_Script()
Draw_Mode_Check()

var i;
for (i = 1; i <= 4; i += 1)
{
    if (joy_button_press[i])
    {
        if (!joystick_check_button(1,i)) joy_button_press[i] = false
    }
}

execute code:if (!joy_button_press[2]) 
{
    joy_button_press[2] = true
    Character_Select()    
}

execute code:if (!joy_button_press[3]) 
{
    joy_button_press[3] = true
    Question_Mark_Display()    
}

{
    if (mouse_x>x and mouse_x<x+sprite_width and mouse_y>y and mouse_y<y+sprite_height and ((!global.big_w_life_draining and !global.big_w_life_giving)or Big_W_Range_Detect()) and instance_number(Level_Cover) == 0 
    and global.Red_B_Killing_Left+global.Red_B_Killing_Up+global.Red_B_Killing_Right+global.Red_B_Killing_Down == 0)
    {
        script_execute(G_Draw,0)
    }
    else 
    {
        if (purple==0) script_execute(G_Draw,1) else script_execute(G_Draw,5)
    }
}
else if (g_type==1) // Gigga G 
{
    if (mouse_x>x and mouse_x<x+71 and mouse_y>y and mouse_y<y+71 and ((!global.big_w_life_draining and !global.big_w_life_giving) or Big_W_Range_Detect()) and instance_number(Level_Cover) == 0 and global.Red_B_Killing_Left+global.Red_B_Killing_Up+global.Red_B_Killing_Right+global.Red_B_Killing_Down == 0) script_execute(G_Draw,0) else script_execute(G_Draw,1)
}
else if (g_type==2) // Terror G
{
    if (mouse_x>x and mouse_x<x+141 and mouse_y>y and mouse_y<y+141 and ((!global.big_w_life_draining and !global.big_w_life_giving) or Big_W_Range_Detect()) and instance_number(Level_Cover) == 0 and global.Red_B_Killing_Left+global.Red_B_Killing_Up+global.Red_B_Killing_Right+global.Red_B_Killing_Down == 0) script_execute(G_Draw,0) else script_execute(G_Draw,1)

Information about object: Player_Name_Room_Check

Sprite: <no sprite>
Solid: false
Visible: true
Depth: 0
Persistent: false
Parent: <no parent>
Mask: <same as sprite>

Create Event:
execute code:keyboard_string = ""
global.MAX_LENGTH = 9

if (global.tablet_mode)
{
    var row key_gap osk_x osk_y;
    row[0] = "1234567890-="
    row[1] = "QWERTYUIOP[]"
    row[2] = "ASDFGHJKL;'"
    row[3] = "ZXCVBNM,./"
    key_gap = grid_size * 2
    osk_x = 175
    osk_y = 315
    var i;
    for (i = 0; i <= 3; i += 1)
    {
        var j;
        for (j = 0; j < string_length(row[i]); j += 1)
        {
            var key;
            key = instance_create((j*key_gap)+osk_x+(grid_size*i), osk_y+(i*key_gap), OSK_Button)
            key.Button_Name = string_char_at(row[i],j+1)
        }
    }
    instance_create(525, 595, OSK_Space) 
    instance_create(osk_x+(key_gap*string_length(row[0])), osk_y, OSK_Backspace)
    instance_create(osk_x+(key_gap*string_length(row[1])), osk_y+(key_gap*2), OSK_Capital)
    instance_create(osk_x+(key_gap*string_length(row[3])+(key_gap*1.5)), osk_y+(key_gap*3), OSK_Symbol)
    with (Player_One_Name_OK)
    {
        x = 980
        y = 630
    }
    with (Player_Two_Name_OK)
    {
        x = 980
        y = 630
    }
}

 Step Event:
execute code:if (string_length(keyboard_string)>global.MAX_LENGTH) keyboard_string = ""

Draw Event:
execute code:draw_set_font(Room_Font)
draw_set_color(c_white)
draw_text(385,140,"Enter Player "+string(global.Player_Name_Change)+" Name: "+string(keyboard_string)+"#"+string("Characters Used: ")+string(string_length(keyboard_string))+string("/")+string(global.MAX_LENGTH))

 Step Event:
execute script Connect_4_Fall with arguments (0,0,0,0,0)
execute code:if (place_meeting(x,y+35,Connect_4_X)) and (place_meeting(x,y+(35*2),Connect_4_X)) and (place_meeting(x,y+(35*3),Connect_4_X))
{
    instance_create(x,y,Red_Vertical_Line)
    script_execute(Line_Get,0)
}

if (global.Connect_4_Falling==0)
{
    if (place_meeting(x+35,y,Connect_4_X)) and (place_meeting(x+(35*2),y,Connect_4_X)) and (place_meeting(x+(35*3),y,Connect_4_X))
    {
        instance_create(x,y,Red_Horizontal_Line)
        script_execute(Line_Get,0)
    }

    if (place_meeting(x+35,y+35,Connect_4_X)) and (place_meeting(x+(35*2),y+(35*2),Connect_4_X)) and (place_meeting(x+(35*3),y+(35*3),Connect_4_X))
    {
        instance_create(x,y,Red_Diagonal_Line_TL_BR)
        script_execute(Line_Get,0)
    }
    if (place_meeting(x-35,y+35,Connect_4_X)) and (place_meeting(x-(35*2),y+(35*2),Connect_4_X)) and (place_meeting(x-(35*3),y+(35*3),Connect_4_X))
    {
        instance_create(x-(35*3),y,Red_Diagonal_Line_TR_BL)
        script_execute(Line_Get,0)
    }
}

Information about object: Connect_4_Control

Sprite: Level_Number_Sprite
Solid: false
Visible: true
Depth: -8
Persistent: false
Parent: <no parent>
Mask: One_Pixel_Sprite

Create Event:
execute code:global.level16messagenumber = 0
global.level16message2hasshown = 0
global.Player_One_Lines = 0
global.Player_Two_Lines = 0

Alarm Event for alarm 0:
execute code:global.Connect_4_Falling = 0

Alarm Event for alarm 1:
execute code:global.mouse_has_clicked = false

 Step Event:
execute script Music_Script with arguments (0,0,0,0,0)
execute script Connect_4_Script with arguments (0,0,0,0,0)

Mouse Event for Glob Left Pressed:
execute code:if (place_meeting(mouse_x,mouse_y,Message_Object))
{
    global.mouse_has_clicked = true
    alarm[1] = 30
}

Mouse Event for Glob Left Released:
execute code:if (place_meeting(mouse_x,mouse_y,Yellow)) and (!(place_meeting(mouse_x,mouse_y,Connect_4_X))) and (!(place_meeting(mouse_x,mouse_y,Connect_4_O))) 
and (!(place_meeting(mouse_x,mouse_y,Connect_4_X_Yellow))) and (!(place_meeting(mouse_x,mouse_y,Connect_4_O_Yellow))) and (global.Connect_4_Falling==0)
and (instance_number(Main_Menu_Button)==0) and (!(place_meeting(mouse_x,mouse_y,Message_Object))) and (!(global.mouse_has_clicked))
{
    if (global.level16messagenumber==0) 
    {
        global.level16messagenumber = 1
        global.message_type = 40
        if (instance_number(Message_Object)==0) instance_create(105,210,Message_Object)
    }
    else
    {
        with(Message_Object) instance_destroy()
    }
    if (instance_number(Connect_4_P1_Turn)>0) 
    {
        instance_create(mouse_x-(mouse_x mod 35),mouse_y-(mouse_y mod 35),Connect_4_X)
        with(Connect_4_P1_Turn) instance_change(Connect_4_P2_Turn,false)
        global.Connect_4_Falling = 1
        alarm[0] = 20
        exit
    }
    if (instance_number(Connect_4_P2_Turn)>0) 
    {
        instance_create(mouse_x-(mouse_x mod 35),mouse_y-(mouse_y mod 35),Connect_4_O)
        with(Connect_4_P2_Turn) instance_change(Connect_4_P1_Turn,false)
        global.Connect_4_Falling = 1
        alarm[0] = 20
        exit
    }
}

Information about object: R_Arrow_Mask

Sprite: Colission_Mask
Solid: false
Visible: true
Depth: 50
Persistent: false
Parent: <no parent>
Mask: <same as sprite>

Alarm Event for alarm 0:
execute code:with(R_Arrow) instance_destroy()

 Step Event:
execute code:// Stefan Grace
// Created: 2018-04-19
// Modified: 2018-04-19

if (x != last_x or y != last_y)
{
    if (instance_number(Go_Number_Black)>0)
    {
        if (place_meeting(x,y,Red_Stuned_Y))
        {
            with(R_Arrow) instance_destroy()
            exit
        }
        with(all)
        {
            if (player == 1)
            {
                if (character_id != 15 and character_id != 13)
                {
                    if (place_meeting(x,y,other))
                    {
                        other.alarm[0] = 1
                        with(R_Arrow) 
                        {
                            hspeed = 0
                            vspeed = 0
                        }
                        instance_destroy()
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }
    else if (instance_number(Go_Number_Red)>0)
    {
        if (place_meeting(x,y,Black_Stuned_Y))
        {
            with(R_Arrow) instance_destroy()
            exit
        }
        with(all)
        {
            if (player == 2)
            {
                if (character_id != 15 and character_id != 13)
                {
                    if (place_meeting(x,y,other))
                    {
                        other.alarm[0] = 1
                        with(R_Arrow) 
                        {
                            hspeed = 0
                            vspeed = 0
                        }
                        instance_destroy()
                    }
                }
            }
        }
    }

}

last_x = x
last_y = y

{
    instance_change(Explosion, true) 
}
else 
{
    instance_destroy()
}

 Step Event:
execute code:with(NWH_To_Be_Exploded)
{
    if ((x - other.x == grid_size*-1 or x - other.x == grid_size) and y - other.y == 0)
    or ((y - other.y == grid_size*-1 or y - other.y == grid_size) and x - other.x == 0)
    {
        if (other.to_be_exploded) to_be_exploded = true
    }
}

Information about object: Switch

Sprite: Switch_Sprite
Solid: false
Visible: true
Depth: -2
Persistent: false
Parent: <no parent>
Mask: <same as sprite>

Create Event:
execute code:instance_create(x,y,Steel)

Mouse Event for Left Released:
execute code:var character_in_range;
character_in_range = false
with(all)
{
    if (player==1 and instance_number(Go_Number_Red)>0)
    or (player==2 and instance_number(Go_Number_Black)>0)
    {
        if place_meeting(x+grid_size,y,other)
        or place_meeting(x-grid_size,y,other) 
        or place_meeting(x,y+grid_size,other)
        or place_meeting(x,y-grid_size,other)
        {
            character_in_range = true;
        } 
    }
}

if (character_in_range)
{
    with(Gate_Object)
    {
        if (gate_id == other.switch_id) Gate_Toggle()
    }
}

Draw Event:
execute code:draw_sprite(Switch_Sprite,0,x,y)

draw_set_halign(fa_center)
draw_set_valign(fa_middle)
draw_set_font(NWH_Font)
draw_text_color(x+17,y+17,switch_id,c_red,c_red,c_red,c_red,1)
draw_set_halign(0)
draw_set_valign(0)

Information about object: Gate_Object

Sprite: Steel_Sprite
Solid: false
Visible: true
Depth: -3
Persistent: false
Parent: <no parent>
Mask: <same as sprite>

Create Event:
execute script Gate_Closed_Create with arguments (0,0,0,0,0)
execute code:instance_create(x,y,Steel)
if (gate_type == 0 or gate_type == 2) instance_create(x,y+(grid_size*((2*gate_size)+1)),Steel)
if (gate_type == 1 or gate_type == 3) instance_create(x+(grid_size*((2*gate_size)+1)),y,Steel)

Draw Event:
execute code:draw_sprite(Steel_Sprite,0,x,y)
if (gate_type == 0 or gate_type == 2) draw_sprite(Steel_Sprite,0,x,y+(grid_size*((2*gate_size)+1)))
if (gate_type == 1 or gate_type == 3) draw_sprite(Steel_Sprite,0,x+(grid_size*((2*gate_size)+1)),y)
draw_set_halign(fa_center)
draw_set_valign(fa_middle)
draw_set_font(NWH_Font)
draw_text_color(x+17,y+17,gate_id,c_red,c_red,c_red,c_red,1)
if (gate_type == 0 or gate_type == 2) draw_text_color(x+17,y+17+(grid_size*((2*gate_size)+1)),gate_id,c_red,c_red,c_red,c_red,1)
if (gate_type == 1 or gate_type == 3) draw_text_color(x+17+(grid_size*((2*gate_size)+1)),y+17,gate_id,c_red,c_red,c_red,c_red,1)
draw_set_halign(0)
draw_set_valign(0)
var i;
if (gate_open)
{
    for (i=grid_size; i<=gate_size*grid_size; i+=grid_size)
    {
        if (gate_type==0) 
        {
            draw_sprite(Gate_Horizontal_Sprite,0,x-i,y+grid_size)
            draw_sprite(Gate_Horizontal_Sprite,0,x-i,y+grid_size+(grid_size*2*gate_size))
        }
        else if (gate_type==1) 
        {
            draw_sprite(Gate_Vertical_Sprite,0,x+grid_size,y-i)
            draw_sprite(Gate_Vertical_Sprite,0,x+grid_size+(grid_size*2*gate_size),y-i)
        }
        else if (gate_type==2) 
        {
            draw_sprite(Gate_Horizontal_Sprite,0,x+i,y+grid_size)
            draw_sprite(Gate_Horizontal_Sprite,0,x+i,y+grid_size+(grid_size*2*gate_size))
        }
        else if (gate_type==3) 
        {
            draw_sprite(Gate_Vertical_Sprite,0,x+grid_size,y+i)
            draw_sprite(Gate_Vertical_Sprite,0,x+grid_size+(grid_size*2*gate_size),y+i)
        }
    }
}
else
{
    for (i=grid_size; i<=gate_size*2*grid_size; i+=grid_size)
    {
        if (gate_type==0) draw_sprite(Gate_Vertical_Sprite,0,x,y+i)
        if (gate_type==1) draw_sprite(Gate_Horizontal_Sprite,0,x+i,y)
        if (gate_type==2) draw_sprite(Gate_Vertical_Sprite,0,x+grid_size,y+i)
        if (gate_type==3) draw_sprite(Gate_Horizontal_Sprite,0,x+i,y+grid_size)
    }
}

Information about object: OSK_Symbol

Sprite: OSK_Normal
Solid: false
Visible: true
Depth: -11
Persistent: false
Parent: <no parent>
Mask: <same as sprite>

Create Event:
execute code:Button_Name = "123 / !@$"

Mouse Event for Left Released:
execute code:symbol = !symbol
var numb symb;
numb = "1234567890-=[];',./"
symb = '!@`$%^&*()_+{}:"<>/'
if (symbol) 
{
    var i;
    for (i = 0; i < string_length(numb); i += 1)
    {
        with (OSK_Button) Button_Name = string_replace_all(Button_Name,string_char_at(numb,i),string_char_at(symb,i))
    }
    
}
else
{
    var i;
    for (i = 0; i < string_length(numb); i += 1)
    {
        with (OSK_Button) Button_Name = string_replace_all(Button_Name,string_char_at(symb,i),string_char_at(numb,i))
    }
    
}

Draw Event:
execute script Button_Text with arguments (4,0,0,0,0)

Information about object: Tablet_UI_Function_Button

Sprite: Player_Random_Sprite
Solid: false
Visible: true
Depth: -10
Persistent: false
Parent: Tablet_UI_Button
Mask: <same as sprite>

 Step Event:
execute code:x = Tablet_UI_Move.x + 30
y = Tablet_UI_Move.y + 200


Mouse Event for Left Released:
execute code:if (instance_number(Tablet_UI) > 0) 
{
    with (Red_Blue) event_perform(ev_keypress, vk_control)
    with (Black_Blue) event_perform(ev_keypress, vk_control)
}

Draw Event:
execute code:if (instance_number(Tablet_UI) > 0)
{
    // Detonate
    if (instance_number(Red_Blue_J) + instance_number(Red_Blue_M) + instance_number(Red_Blue_Z) + instance_number(Red_Blue_T) > 0)
    {
        draw_set_font(Player_Select_Font)
        draw_set_color(c_red)
        draw_set_halign(fa_center)
        draw_set_valign(fa_center)
        draw_sprite(Player_One_Sprite,0,x,y)
        draw_text(x+(sprite_width/2),y+(sprite_height/2),global.text_detonate)
        draw_set_halign(0)
        draw_set_valign(0)
    }
    else if (instance_number(Black_Blue_J) + instance_number(Black_Blue_M) + instance_number(Black_Blue_Z) + instance_number(Black_Blue_T) > 0)
    {
        draw_set_font(Player_Select_Font)
        draw_set_color(c_black)
        draw_set_halign(fa_center)
        draw_set_valign(fa_center)
        draw_sprite(Player_Two_Sprite,0,x,y)
        draw_text(x+(sprite_width/2),y+(sprite_height/2),global.text_detonate)
        draw_set_halign(0)
        draw_set_valign(0)
    }
    // Cast
    else if (instance_number(Red_Blue_W) + instance_number(Red_Blue_Dollar_Sign) > 0)
    {
        draw_set_font(Player_Select_Font)
        draw_set_color(c_red)
        draw_set_halign(fa_center)
        draw_set_valign(fa_center)
        draw_sprite(Player_One_Sprite,0,x,y)
        draw_text(x+(sprite_width/2),y+(sprite_height/2),global.text_cast)
        draw_set_halign(0)
        draw_set_valign(0)
    }
    else if (instance_number(Black_Blue_W) + instance_number(Black_Blue_Dollar_Sign) > 0)
    {
        draw_set_font(Player_Select_Font)
        draw_set_color(c_black)
        draw_set_halign(fa_center)
        draw_set_valign(fa_center)
        draw_sprite(Player_Two_Sprite,0,x,y)
        draw_text(x+(sprite_width/2),y+(sprite_height/2),global.text_cast)
        draw_set_halign(0)
        draw_set_valign(0)
    }
    // Swap
    else if (instance_number(Red_Blue_At)> 0)
    {
        draw_set_font(Player_Select_Font)
        draw_set_color(c_red)
        draw_set_halign(fa_center)
        draw_set_valign(fa_center)
        draw_sprite(Player_One_Sprite,0,x,y)
        draw_text(x+(sprite_width/2),y+(sprite_height/2),global.text_swap)
        draw_set_halign(0)
        draw_set_valign(0)
    }
    else if (instance_number(Black_Blue_At)> 0)
    {
        draw_set_font(Player_Select_Font)
        draw_set_color(c_black)
        draw_set_halign(fa_center)
        draw_set_valign(fa_center)
        draw_sprite(Player_Two_Sprite,0,x,y)
        draw_text(x+(sprite_width/2),y+(sprite_height/2),global.text_swap)
        draw_set_halign(0)
        draw_set_valign(0)
    }
    // Spawn
    else if (instance_number(Red_Blue_Q)> 0)
    {
        draw_set_font(Player_Select_Font)
        draw_set_color(c_red)
        draw_set_halign(fa_center)
        draw_set_valign(fa_center)
        draw_sprite(Player_One_Sprite,0,x,y)
        draw_text(x+(sprite_width/2),y+(sprite_height/2),global.text_spawn)
        draw_set_halign(0)
        draw_set_valign(0)
    }
    else if (instance_number(Black_Blue_Q)> 0)
    {
        draw_set_font(Player_Select_Font)
        draw_set_color(c_black)
        draw_set_halign(fa_center)
        draw_set_valign(fa_center)
        draw_sprite(Player_Two_Sprite,0,x,y)
        draw_text(x+(sprite_width/2),y+(sprite_height/2),global.text_spawn)
        draw_set_halign(0)
        draw_set_valign(0)
    }
}
